","\\hline\\hline\\endhead \\hline\\hline\\endfoot","    \\texttt{perror()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{void perror(const char* s)} --- Prints \\texttt{s} and syscall's error message as defined by global int \\texttt{errno} to \\texttt{stderr}. If syscall has error, \\texttt{errno} is changed. Technically not a syscall.","        %","        \\\\ ","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{stdio.h}, \\texttt{errno.h}","        \\\\ \\hline%\\cline{1-1}\\tabucline[2pt]{-}","    % fork","    \\texttt{fork()} \u0026  \\indenth\\texttt{pid\\_t fork()} --- Creates child process. Returns \\texttt{0} to child process and child's process id to parent process or \\texttt{-1} if error. No child process made if error occurs.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","    %","    % exec","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}%\\hline","    \\texttt{exec} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{Exec} note: If \\texttt{exec} succeeds, the current process will end and \\texttt{exec} will not return. It returns \\texttt{-1} if it fails (e.g. program file not found). \\texttt{char *const argv} must be \\texttt{NULL} terminated. \\par","        \\\\ ","    \\texttt{execv()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int execv(const char* path, char *const argv[])} --- Executes program \\texttt{path} and passes arguments \\texttt{argv}. Requires full path name of program.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        \\\\","    \\texttt{execvp()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int execvp(const char* file, char *const argv[])} --- Executes program \\texttt{path} and passes arguments \\texttt{argv}. Finds file automatically by checking directories in environmental variable \\texttt{PATH}.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","    %","    % wait","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}%\\cline{2-2}%\\hline","    \\texttt{wait()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{pid\\_t wait(int* status)} --- Waits for child process to terminate. \\texttt{int* status} stores exit status of child process. Use \\texttt{NULL} if not needed. Returns child pid if succeeds, \\texttt{-1} if fails (e.g. no child). ","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/wait.h}","    %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{waitpid()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{pid\\_t waitpid(pid\\_t pid, int* status, int options)} --- Similar to \\texttt{wait()}. Can specify \\texttt{pid} to wait for specific child; use 0 for any child. Can also wait for stopped processes by adding option \\texttt{WUNTRACED} and check immediately instead of waiting with \\texttt{WNOHANG} (Bitwise OR to combine: '\\texttt{WUNTRACED | WNOHANG}'). Returns child pid if succeeds, \\texttt{-1} if fails (e.g. invalid pid).","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/wait.h}","    % opendir","        \\\\ \\hline","    Directories and Files \u0026 \\indenth Note: When these functions require a directory or file name, they only require a \\itshape relative path\\rm. This means that if your process was called in directory \\texttt{bin/foo/bar/}, instead of using \\texttt{bin/foo/bar/p.cpp}, the \\itshape absolute path\\rm,  you can use \\texttt{p.cpp} or \\texttt{./p.cpp} instead. \\par","        \\\\ %\\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}","    \\texttt{opendir()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{DIR* opendir(const char* name)} --- Opens directory stream to directory \\texttt{name} and returns pointer to its first entry. Returns \\texttt{NULL} on error. ","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{dirent.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{closedir()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int closedir(DIR* dirp)} --- Closes  directory. returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{dirent.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}","    \\texttt{chdir()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int chdir(const char* path)} --- Change directory of calling process to \\texttt{path}. Returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/stat.h}, \\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}","    \\texttt{stat()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int stat(const char* path,  struct stat* buf)} --- Gives information about a file in \\texttt{struct stat}, e.g. permissions, type of file, time created. See \\texttt{ls -l} for example of provided information. Macros are also provided that take \\texttt{mode\\_t st\\_mode} in \\texttt{struct stat} and returns \\texttt{true}/\\texttt{false} (e.g. \\texttt{S\\_ISDIR(st\\_mode)}, \\texttt{S\\_REG(st\\_mode)}). Returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/types.h}, \\texttt{sys/stat.h}, \\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\hline","    \\texttt{open()} \u0026 \\texttt{int open(const char* pathname, int flags)}","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\texttt{int open(const char* pathname, int flags, mod\\_t mode)}","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\indenth\\hspace{.5in}Opens file and returns file descriptor which can be used, with flags, to read/write/create file. ","    \\newline\\textbf{Flags:} Must use either \\texttt{O\\_RDONLY} (read file), \\texttt{O\\_WRONLY} (write to file), or \\texttt{O\\_RDWR} (both) in call. These can be bitwise \\texttt{OR}'d ('\\texttt{O\\_WRONLY | O\\_CREAT}') with other flags such as:  \\texttt{O\\_CREAT} creates file if it doesn't exist. \\texttt{O\\_TRUNC} overwrites contents of file when writing, \\texttt{O\\_APPEND} writes at the end of file instead. ","    \\newline\\textbf{Modes:} When creating files, \\texttt{mode} arguments can be added to specify permissions of new file, such as \\texttt{S\\_IRWXU} - user has read/write/execute permission, \\texttt{S\\_IRUSR} - user has read permission, or \\texttt{S\\_IWUSR} - user has read permission.","    \\newline\\textbf{Warning:} Every call to \\texttt{open()} must have a corresponding \\texttt{close()} or else file descriptors will be left open (similar to memory leaks with \\texttt{new} and \\texttt{delete}).","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/types.h}, \\texttt{sys/stat.h}, \\texttt{fcntl.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{close()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int close(int fd)} --- Close file descriptor. Returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error (e.g. invalid fd).","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\hline","    \\texttt{dup()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int dup(int oldfd)} --- Copies file descriptor \\texttt{oldfd} to the next lowest unused descriptor, returns new file descriptor on success, \\texttt{-1} if error.","    \\newline\\hspace{.5in}\\textbf{Warning:} be sure to close copies after you finish using them. File descriptors are limited.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{dup2()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int dup2(int oldfd, int newfd)} --- Copies file descriptor \\texttt{oldfd} in \\texttt{newfd}. Closes \\texttt{newfd} if it already exists. Returns new file descriptor on success, \\texttt{-1} if error","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{pipe()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int pipe(int pipefd[2])} --- Returns two file descriptors in \\texttt{pipefd} for reading from and writing to. The file descriptors are one way pipes only, hence the need for two. Data written to \\texttt{pipefd[1]} can be read from \\texttt{pipefd[0]}. \\texttt{pipe} is usually associated with piping in bash. ","    \\newline\\hspace{.5in}e.g. \\texttt{ls | grep .cpp}. ","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\hline","    Useful Signals \u0026 \\texttt{SIGINT} to interrupt (\\texttt{Ctrl+c}), \\texttt{SIGTSTP} to temporarily stop (\\texttt{Ctrl+z}), or \\texttt{SIGQUIT} to quit (\\texttt{Ctrl+\\textbackslash}). \\par","        \\\\","    \\texttt{signal()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{sighandler\\_t signal(int signum, sighandler\\_t handler)} --- Sets signal handler for signal \\texttt{signum} to function \\texttt{handler}.  For signal handlers: \\texttt{SIG\\_IGN} ignores signal and \\texttt{SIG\\_DFL} uses default handler. You can also use a user-defined handler as an argument. \\texttt{sighandler\\_t} is a pointer to a void function that has an int parameter: \\texttt{void myhandler(int sig)}","    \\newline\\hspace{.5in}e.g. \\texttt{signal(SIGINT, myhandler);}","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{signal.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}","    \\texttt{sigaction()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int sigaction(int signum, const struct sigaction *act, struct sigaction *oldact)} ","        \\\\ ","    \u0026 \\indenth\\hspace{.5in}Similar to \\texttt{signal()}, but is more portable and conforms to POSIX. Not needed for CS100 projects. Sets signal handler of signal \\texttt{signum} to handler specified in members \\texttt{sa\\_handler} or \\texttt{sa\\_sigaction} of \\texttt{struct sigaction act} and saves old handler struct to \\texttt{oldact}.  You can leave \\texttt{act} or \\texttt{old} \\texttt{NULL}.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{signal.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}","    \\texttt{kill()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int kill(pid\\_t pid, int sig)} --- Sends any signal to process or proccess group. Returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/types.h}, \\texttt{signal.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\hline","    \\texttt{getcwd()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{char* getcwd(char*buf, size\\_t size)} --- Returns pointer to current working directory string on success and copies to \\texttt{buf} of size \\texttt{size} if not \\texttt{NULL}.  Returns \\texttt{NULL} if error.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{gethostname()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int gethostname(char* name, size\\_t len)} --- Writes hostname (\\texttt{hammer.cs.ucr.edu}) to char array \\texttt{name} with size \\texttt{len}.  According to the man page, the guaranteed maximum value for \\texttt{len} is \\texttt{HOST\\_NAME\\_MAX = 64}, which is in \\texttt{limits.h}. Returns \\texttt{0} on success, \\texttt{-1} if error. \\newline\\hspace{.5in}Note: \\texttt{char} array must be large enough to hold hostname and \\texttt{NULL} char.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ ","    \\texttt{getlogin()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{char* getlogin()} --- Returns pointer to current user's username on success, NULL if error. Do not \\texttt{delete} pointer as string is static. This also means changing the string will change return value of subsequent calls to \\texttt{getlogin()}.","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{unistd.h}","        %","        \\\\ ","    \\texttt{getgrgid()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{struct group* getgrgid(gid\\_t gid)} --- Returns pointer to struct with group information on success, NULL on not finding group id \\texttt{gid} or error (set \\texttt{errno} to \\texttt{0} before syscall, then check \\texttt{errno} to tell which). ","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/types.h}, \\texttt{grp.h}","        %","        \\\\","    \\texttt{getpwuid()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{struct passwd* getpwuid(uid\\_t uid)} --- Returns pointer to struct with user information associated with \\texttt{uid} or \\texttt{NULL} if error occurs or \\texttt{uid} not found (set \\texttt{errno} to \\texttt{0} before syscall, then check \\texttt{errno} to tell which).","        \\\\","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/types.h}, \\texttt{pwd.h}","        %","        \\\\ \\hline","    \\texttt{ioctl()} \u0026 \\indenth\\texttt{int ioctl(int d, int request, ...)} --- Sends request to file descriptor \\texttt{d}.  Used to manipulate devices and terminals. Returns \\texttt{0} on success usually (some devices use return as output value), \\texttt{-1} on error. Request codes are different for each device and so no example is listed here. The third parameter is traditionally a \\texttt{char* argp}. ","        \\\\ ","    \u0026 \\hspace{.5in}\\it Include: \\rm\\texttt{sys/ioctl.h}","        \\\\ Returns \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\texttt\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e} on success usually (some devices use return as output value), \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\texttt\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-1\u003c/span\u003e} on error. Request codes are different for each device and so no example is listed here. The third parameter is traditionally a \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\texttt\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003echar* argp\u003c/span\u003e}. ","        \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003e ","    \u0026amp; \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\hspace\u003c/span\u003e{.5in}\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\it\u003c/span\u003e Include: \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\rm\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\texttt\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003esys/ioctl.h\u003c/span\u003e}","        \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\\\\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\hline\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\end\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003elongtabu\u003c/span\u003e}","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\\end\u003c/span\u003e{\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003edocument\u003c/span\u003e}","",""]}},"title":"ucr-cs100/textbook/cheatsheets/Syscall_cheatsheet.tex at 2015winter · mikeizbicki/ucr-cs100","appPayload":{},"meta":{"title":"ucr-cs100/textbook/cheatsheets/Syscall_cheatsheet.tex at 2015winter · mikeizbicki/ucr-cs100"}}</script>

<div id="LC34" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">document</span>}</div>
<div id="LC35" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC36" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\huge</span> CS100 Syscall Cheatsheet</div>
<div id="LC37" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">
</div>
<div id="LC38" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\bigskip\it\large</span> Read your man pages, and sleep once in a while, k?<span class="pl-c1">\rm</span></div>
<div id="LC39" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC40" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">
</div>
<div id="LC41" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\normalsize</span></div>
<div id="LC42" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">longtabu</span>}{|[1pt]p{.9in}|p{6.3in}&lt;{<span class="pl-c1">\strut</span>}|[1pt]} </div>
<div id="LC43" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\hline\hline\endhead</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline\hline\endfoot</span></div>
<div id="LC44" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">perror()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">void perror(const char* s)</span>} --- Prints <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">s</span>} and syscall&#39;s error message as defined by global int <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">errno</span>} to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">stderr</span>}. If syscall has error, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">errno</span>} is changed. Technically not a syscall.</div>
<div id="LC45" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC46" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> </div>
<div id="LC47" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">stdio.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">errno.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC48" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\cline{1-1}\tabucline[2pt]{-}</span></div>
<div id="LC49" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> fork</span></div>
<div id="LC50" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">fork()</span>} &amp;  <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pid<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t fork()</span>} --- Creates child process. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} to child process and child&#39;s process id to parent process or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error. No child process made if error occurs.</div>
<div id="LC51" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC52" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC53" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC54" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> exec</span></div>
<div id="LC55" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC56" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">exec</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">Exec</span>} note: If <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">exec</span>} succeeds, the current process will end and <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">exec</span>} will not return. It returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if it fails (e.g. program file not found). <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">char *const argv</span>} must be <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>} terminated. <span class="pl-c1">\par</span></div>
<div id="LC57" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> </div>
<div id="LC58" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">execv()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int execv(const char* path, char *const argv[])</span>} --- Executes program <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">path</span>} and passes arguments <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">argv</span>}. Requires full path name of program.</div>
<div id="LC59" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC60" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC61" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC62" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">execvp()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int execvp(const char* file, char *const argv[])</span>} --- Executes program <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">path</span>} and passes arguments <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">argv</span>}. Finds file automatically by checking directories in environmental variable <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">PATH</span>}.</div>
<div id="LC63" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC64" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC65" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC66" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> wait</span></div>
<div id="LC67" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\cline{2-2}%\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC68" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">wait()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pid<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t wait(int* status)</span>} --- Waits for child process to terminate. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int* status</span>} stores exit status of child process. Use <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>} if not needed. Returns child pid if succeeds, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if fails (e.g. no child). </div>
<div id="LC69" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC70" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/wait.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC71" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC72" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC73" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">waitpid()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pid<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t waitpid(pid<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t pid, int* status, int options)</span>} --- Similar to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">wait()</span>}. Can specify <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pid</span>} to wait for specific child; use 0 for any child. Can also wait for stopped processes by adding option <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">WUNTRACED</span>} and check immediately instead of waiting with <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">WNOHANG</span>} (Bitwise OR to combine: <span class="pl-ii">&#39;\texttt{WUNTRACED | WNOHANG}&#39;</span>). Returns child pid if succeeds, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if fails (e.g. invalid pid).</div>
<div id="LC74" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC75" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/wait.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC76" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> opendir</span></div>
<div id="LC77" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC78" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    Directories and Files &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span> Note: When these functions require a directory or file name, they only require a <span class="pl-c1">\itshape</span> relative path<span class="pl-c1">\rm</span>. This means that if your process was called in directory <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">bin/foo/bar/</span>}, instead of using <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">bin/foo/bar/p.cpp</span>}, the <span class="pl-c1">\itshape</span> absolute path<span class="pl-c1">\rm</span>,  you can use <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">p.cpp</span>} or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">./p.cpp</span>} instead. <span class="pl-c1">\par</span></div>
<div id="LC79" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\tabucline[.3pt]{2-2}</span></div>
<div id="LC80" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">opendir()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">DIR* opendir(const char* name)</span>} --- Opens directory stream to directory <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">name</span>} and returns pointer to its first entry. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>} on error. </div>
<div id="LC81" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC82" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">dirent.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC83" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC84" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC85" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">closedir()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int closedir(DIR* dirp)</span>} --- Closes  directory. returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error.</div>
<div id="LC86" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC87" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">dirent.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC88" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC89" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}</div>
<div id="LC90" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">chdir()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int chdir(const char* path)</span>} --- Change directory of calling process to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">path</span>}. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error.</div>
<div id="LC91" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC92" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/stat.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC93" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC94" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}</div>
<div id="LC95" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">stat()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int stat(const char* path,  struct stat* buf)</span>} --- Gives information about a file in <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">struct stat</span>}, e.g. permissions, type of file, time created. See <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">ls -l</span>} for example of provided information. Macros are also provided that take <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">mode<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t st<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>mode</span>} in <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">struct stat</span>} and returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">true</span>}/<span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">false</span>} (e.g. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">S<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>ISDIR(st<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>mode)</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">S<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>REG(st<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>mode)</span>}). Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error.</div>
<div id="LC96" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC97" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/types.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/stat.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC98" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC99" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC100" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">open()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int open(const char* pathname, int flags)</span>}</div>
<div id="LC101" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC102" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int open(const char* pathname, int flags, mod<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t mode)</span>}</div>
<div id="LC103" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC104" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth\hspace</span>{.5in}Opens file and returns file descriptor which can be used, with flags, to read/write/create file. </div>
<div id="LC105" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline</span><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Flags:</span>} Must use either <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>RDONLY</span>} (read file), <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>WRONLY</span>} (write to file), or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>RDWR</span>} (both) in call. These can be bitwise <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">OR</span>}&#39;d (&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>WRONLY | O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>CREAT</span>}&#39;) with other flags such as:  <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>CREAT</span>} creates file if it doesn&#39;t exist. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>TRUNC</span>} overwrites contents of file when writing, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">O<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>APPEND</span>} writes at the end of file instead. </div>
<div id="LC106" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline</span><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Modes:</span>} When creating files, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">mode</span>} arguments can be added to specify permissions of new file, such as <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">S<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>IRWXU</span>} - user has read/write/execute permission, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">S<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>IRUSR</span>} - user has read permission, or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">S<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>IWUSR</span>} - user has read permission.</div>
<div id="LC107" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline</span><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Warning:</span>} Every call to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">open()</span>} must have a corresponding <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">close()</span>} or else file descriptors will be left open (similar to memory leaks with <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">new</span>} and <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">delete</span>}).</div>
<div id="LC108" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC109" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/types.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/stat.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">fcntl.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC110" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC111" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC112" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">close()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int close(int fd)</span>} --- Close file descriptor. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error (e.g. invalid fd).</div>
<div id="LC113" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC114" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC115" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC116" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC117" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">dup()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int dup(int oldfd)</span>} --- Copies file descriptor <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">oldfd</span>} to the next lowest unused descriptor, returns new file descriptor on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error.</div>
<div id="LC118" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Warning:</span>} be sure to close copies after you finish using them. File descriptors are limited.</div>
<div id="LC119" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC120" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC121" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC122" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC123" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">dup2()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int dup2(int oldfd, int newfd)</span>} --- Copies file descriptor <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">oldfd</span>} in <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">newfd</span>}. Closes <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">newfd</span>} if it already exists. Returns new file descriptor on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error</div>
<div id="LC124" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC125" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC126" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC127" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC128" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pipe()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int pipe(int pipefd[2])</span>} --- Returns two file descriptors in <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pipefd</span>} for reading from and writing to. The file descriptors are one way pipes only, hence the need for two. Data written to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pipefd[1]</span>} can be read from <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pipefd[0]</span>}. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">pipe</span>} is usually associated with piping in bash. </div>
<div id="LC129" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline\hspace</span>{.5in}e.g. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">ls | grep .cpp</span>}. </div>
<div id="LC130" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC131" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">unistd.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC132" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC133" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\hline</span></div>
<div id="LC134" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    Useful Signals &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">SIGINT</span>} to interrupt (<span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">Ctrl+c</span>}), <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">SIGTSTP</span>} to temporarily stop (<span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">Ctrl+z</span>}), or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">SIGQUIT</span>} to quit (<span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">Ctrl+<span class="pl-c1">\textbackslash</span></span>}). <span class="pl-c1">\par</span></div>
<div id="LC135" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC136" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sighandler<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t signal(int signum, sighandler<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t handler)</span>} --- Sets signal handler for signal <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signum</span>} to function <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">handler</span>}.  For signal handlers: <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">SIG<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>IGN</span>} ignores signal and <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">SIG<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>DFL</span>} uses default handler. You can also use a user-defined handler as an argument. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sighandler<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t</span>} is a pointer to a void function that has an int parameter: <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">void myhandler(int sig)</span>}</div>
<div id="LC137" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\newline\hspace</span>{.5in}e.g. <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal(SIGINT, myhandler);</span>}</div>
<div id="LC138" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC139" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC140" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC141" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}</div>
<div id="LC142" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sigaction()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int sigaction(int signum, const struct sigaction *act, struct sigaction *oldact)</span>} </div>
<div id="LC143" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> </div>
<div id="LC144" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth\hspace</span>{.5in}Similar to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal()</span>}, but is more portable and conforms to POSIX. Not needed for CS100 projects. Sets signal handler of signal <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signum</span>} to handler specified in members <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sa<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>handler</span>} or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sa<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>sigaction</span>} of <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">struct sigaction act</span>} and saves old handler struct to <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">oldact</span>}.  You can leave <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">act</span>} or <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">old</span>} <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>}.</div>
<div id="LC145" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC146" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal.h</span>}</div>
<div id="LC147" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span></span></div>
<div id="LC148" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span> <span class="pl-c1">\tabucline</span>[.3pt]{2-2}</div>
<div id="LC149" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">kill()</span>} &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\indenth</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">int kill(pid<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>t pid, int sig)</span>} --- Sends any signal to process or proccess group. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error.</div>
<div id="LC150" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">        <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC151" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">    &amp; <span class="pl-c1">\hspace</span>{.5in}<span class="pl-c1">\it</span> Include: <span class="pl-c1">\rm</span><span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">sys/types.h</span>}, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">signal.h</span>}</div>

Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success, <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} if error. <span class="pl-c1">\newline\hspace</span>{.5in}Note: <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">char</span>} array must be large enough to hold hostname and <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">NULL</span>} char.</div>

Used to manipulate devices and terminals. Returns <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">0</span>} on success usually (some devices use return as output value), <span class="pl-c1">\texttt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">-1</span>} on error.
